                        <span style="padding-left: 5px;">
                            <strong style="font-size:15pt;">Kenta Maeda</strong></span>

                    <tr style="background-color: #FFF;"><td style="border-top:2px solid #D3D3D3; font-size:10pt;"><div style="padding-top:5px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:5px;"><b><a href="http://www.rotowire.com/users/ad_jump.asp?id=688&playerid=12051" style="text-decoration:none;">RotoWire News</a>:</b> Maeda (9-4) yielded two runs (one earned) over five innings in a win over the Twins on Tuesday. He struck out four while giving up five hits and two walks. (7/26/2017)</div></td></tr>

                <tr style="background-color: #FFF;"><td style="border-top:2px solid #D3D3D3; vertical-align:top; padding-bottom:4px; padding-left:5px;"><div class="m_stories" style="font-size:13pt"><span class="m_date">7/29/2017</span> - <a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/fantasy/the-sleeper-and-the-bust-episode-462-sp-ranking-updates/">The Sleeper and the Bust Episode: 462 – SP Ranking&raquo;</a><span class="m_comments"> by </span><span class="m_author"><a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/fantasy/index.php?author=11752">Paul Sporer (RotoGraphs)</a></span><span class="m_comments">&nbsp;<a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/fantasy/the-sleeper-and-the-bust-episode-462-sp-ranking-updates/#comments"><img src="images/commentslink.gif" border="0px" />10</a></span><br /><span class="m_date">5/22/2017</span> - <a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/blogs/its-time-for-a-pitcher-to-throw-80-breaking-balls/">It's Time for a Pitcher to Throw 80% Breaking Ball&raquo;</a><span class="m_comments"> by </span><span class="m_author"><a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/blogs/index.php?author=22">Eno Sarris (FanGraphs)</a></span><span class="m_comments">&nbsp;<a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/blogs/its-time-for-a-pitcher-to-throw-80-breaking-balls/#comments"><img src="images/commentslink.gif" border="0px" />39</a></span><br /><span class="m_date">5/17/2017</span> - <a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/blogs/everyone-is-on-the-disabled-list-right-now/">Everyone Is on the Disabled List Right Now</a><span class="m_comments"> by </span><span class="m_author"><a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/blogs/index.php?author=22">Eno Sarris (FanGraphs)</a></span><span class="m_comments">&nbsp;<a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/blogs/everyone-is-on-the-disabled-list-right-now/#comments"><img src="images/commentslink.gif" border="0px" />29</a></span><br /></div></td></tr>

                <tr id="so1" style="background-color: #FFF;"><td colspan="5" style="border-top:2px solid #D3D3D3; padding:3px; text-align:justify;"><div class="m_stories" style="width:100%; font-size:10pt"><center>Profiles:&nbsp;&nbsp;<a id="soa8" href="javascript:showMoreSO2016();">2016</a>&nbsp;&nbsp;<a id="soa9"  href="javascript:showMoreSO2017();">2017</a>&nbsp;&nbsp;(Click Year to Expand / <a href="javascript:hideSO('so1');">Close</a>)</center></div></td></tr>
                
                
                
                
                
                
                <tr id="so8" style="background-color: #FFF; display:none;"><td colspan="5" padding:3px; text-align:justify;"><div class="m_stories" style="font-size:10pt"><center><table><tr><td style="width:615px; padding-right:7px; text-align:justify;" valign="top"><b>Profile: </b>Maeda has good location of all four of his pitches, with his fastball and slider having the best command and highest impact. His success hinges on his fastball command, since he doesn’t have the pure arm strength to just pump into the zone.  His slider may be the only pitch that ends up grading out above-average, and it’s not even much about how sharp it is. He has an awesome ability to spot it low to his glove side consistently, getting under the barrels of both righties and lefties. His curve and changeup are less advanced stuff-wise, but his feel for when and how to throw them both are superb. His plus command is what gets him most of the way to his number-three-starter status, though his arsenal is sneaky effective even when he misses spots. (Dan Farnsworth)<br /><br /><b>The Quick Opinion: </b>Maeda will succeed where most Japanese pitchers have not in the transition to American baseball by maintaining his low walk rate. His command is really impressive, and even when his stuff isn’t at its peak he can get guys out with superior location.</td></tr></table></center></div></td></tr>
                <tr id="so9" style="background-color: #FFF; display:none;"><td colspan="5" padding:3px; text-align:justify;"><div class="m_stories" style="font-size:10pt"><center><table><tr><td style="width:615px; padding-right:7px; text-align:justify;" valign="top"><b>Profile: </b>Like many other Japanese pitchers, Maeda has an increased injury risk as a result of the differing pitching philosophies between NPB and MLB. Fortunately, he hasn’t displayed any red flags with the Dodgers, so it isn’t an immediate problem. We knew Maeda would have great command, it is his greatest strength. He walked only 7% of the batters he faced in 2016, so no surprise there. However, generating a 25% strikeout rate, 14th best in MLB, might have been a surprise. If not, how about his 12% swinging strike rate—tied for 12th best? Perhaps most amazing of all, Maeda had the second lowest average exit velocity of all qualified pitchers with 85.7 mph, 3.1 mph below average. So let's set this straight: 14th best K%, 12th best SwStrk%, 2nd lowest Exit Velocity. These are the stats of an overpowering ace. His ERA jumped from 3.28 to 3.48 during his final start, otherwise he would have finished in the top 20 in that category as well. There is risk, though. His sinker, a pitch he has relied on for ground balls, is average and could be taken advantage of. Batters refuse to swing at his curveball, which is a below average pitch. There is risk that major league batters will make adjustments that can punish Maeda. That brings me back to his greatest strength: command. He doesn’t have the velocity or movement to venture far from the corners of the zone.(Andrew Perpetua)<br /><br /><b>The Quick Opinion: </b>Some believed Kenta Maeda could match Tanaka’s success in MLB, which felt like a stretch at the time. As it turns out, those people were right. Kenta Maeda is an ace, but with an ace price tag he also carries significant risk. If his command slips things can get ugly in a hurry.</td></tr></table></center></div></td></tr>
            </table>
        </td>
        <td style="width: 302px; height: 250px; vertical-align: top;">

        </td>
    </tr>
</table>

    function showMoreSO() {
        //    var panel = document.getElementById('so1');

    function setAverage(t) {
        var elements;
        var browserCheck = (document.all) ? 1 : 0;
        if (t == '*') {
            elements = (ie) ? document.all : document.getElementsByTagName('*');
        } else {
            elements = document.getElementsByTagName(t);
        }
        for (var i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) {
            var node = elements.item(i);
            var vis = elements.item(i).style;
            for (var j = 0; j < node.attributes.length; j++) {
                if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeName == 'class') {
                    if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeValue == 'rgRow grid_average') {


                        if (browserCheck > 0) {

                            if (vis.display == undefined) {
                                vis.dispaly = 'block';
                            }
                            else {
                                if (vis.display == 'block') { vis.display = 'none'; } else { vis.display = 'block'; }
                            }

                        }

                        else {

                            if (vis.display == undefined) {
                                vis.dispaly = 'table-row';
                            }
                            else {
                                if (vis.display == 'table-row') { vis.display = 'none'; } else { vis.display = 'table-row'; }
                            }

                        }

                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    function setPost(t) {
        var elements;
        var browserCheck = (document.all) ? 1 : 0;
        if (t == '*') {
            elements = (ie) ? document.all : document.getElementsByTagName('*');
        } else {
            elements = document.getElementsByTagName(t);
        }
        for (var i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) {
            var node = elements.item(i);
            var vis = elements.item(i).style;
            for (var j = 0; j < node.attributes.length; j++) {
                if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeName == 'class') {
                    if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeValue == 'rgRow grid_postseason' || node.attributes.item(j).nodeValue == 'rgRow grid_postseason_total') {


                        if (browserCheck > 0) {

                            if (vis.display == undefined) {
                                vis.dispaly = 'block';
                            }
                            else {
                                if (vis.display == 'block') { vis.display = 'none'; } else { vis.display = 'block'; }
                            }

                        }

                        else {

                            if (vis.display == undefined) {
                                vis.dispaly = 'table-row';
                            }
                            else {
                                if (vis.display == 'table-row') { vis.display = 'none'; } else { vis.display = 'table-row'; }
                            }

                        }

                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    function setProj(t) {
        var elements;
        var browserCheck = (document.all) ? 1 : 0;
        if (t == '*') {
            elements = (ie) ? document.all : document.getElementsByTagName('*');
        } else {
            elements = document.getElementsByTagName(t);
        }
        for (var i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) {
            var node = elements.item(i);
            var vis = elements.item(i).style;
            for (var j = 0; j < node.attributes.length; j++) {
                if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeName == 'class') {
                    if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeValue == 'rgRow grid_projections_show') {

                        if (browserCheck > 0) {

                            if (vis.display == 'none') {
                                vis.display = 'block';
                            }
                            else {
                                vis.display = 'none';
                            }

                        }

                        else {

                            if (vis.display == 'none') {
                                vis.display = 'table-row';
                            }
                            else {
                                vis.display = 'none';
                            }

                        }

                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    function setRegular(t) {
        var elements;
        var browserCheck = (document.all) ? 1 : 0;
        if (t == '*') {
            elements = (ie) ? document.all : document.getElementsByTagName('*');
        } else {
            elements = document.getElementsByTagName(t);
        }
        for (var i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) {
            var node = elements.item(i);
            var vis = elements.item(i).style;
            for (var j = 0; j < node.attributes.length; j++) {
                if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeName == 'class') {
                    if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeValue == 'rgRow' || node.attributes.item(j).nodeValue == 'rgAltRow' || node.attributes.item(j).nodeValue == 'rgRow grid_total') {

                        if (browserCheck > 0) {

                            if (vis.display == 'none') {
                                vis.display = 'block';
                            }
                            else {
                                vis.display = 'none';
                            }

                        }

                        else {

                            if (vis.display == 'none') {
                                vis.display = 'table-row';
                            }
                            else {
                                vis.display = 'none';
                            }

                        }

                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    function setPart(t) {
        var elements;
        var browserCheck = (document.all) ? 1 : 0;
        if (t == '*') {
            elements = (ie) ? document.all : document.getElementsByTagName('*');
        } else {
            elements = document.getElementsByTagName(t);
        }
        for (var i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) {
            var node = elements.item(i);
            var vis = elements.item(i).style;
            for (var j = 0; j < node.attributes.length; j++) {
                if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeName == 'class') {
                    if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeValue == 'rgRow grid_multi' || node.attributes.item(j).nodeValue == 'rgRow grid_multi') {


                        if (browserCheck > 0) {

                            if (vis.display == undefined) {
                                vis.dispaly = 'block';
                            }
                            else {
                                if (vis.display == 'block') { vis.display = 'none'; } else { vis.display = 'block'; }
                            }

                        }

                        else {

                            if (vis.display == undefined) {
                                vis.dispaly = 'table-row';
                            }
                            else {
                                if (vis.display == 'table-row') { vis.display = 'none'; } else { vis.display = 'table-row'; }
                            }

                        }

                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    // Create the tooltips only on document load
    $(document).ready(function () {
        // Make sure to only match links to wikipedia with a rel tag
        $('a[tipgloss]').each(function () {
            // We make use of the .each() loop to gain access to each element via the "this" keyword...
            $(this).qtip(
		{
		    content: {
		        // Set the text to an image HTML string with the correct src URL to the loading image you want to use
		        text: " ",
		        ajax: {
		            url: $(this).attr('tipgloss') // Use the rel attribute of each element for the url to load
		        }
		    },
		    position: {
		        viewport: $(window),
		        at: "top center",
		        my: "bottom center",
		        effect: false
		    },
		    show: {
		        event: "click mouseenter",
		        solo: true // Only show one tooltip at a time
		    },
		    hide: {
		        event: "click mouseleave",
		        delay: 1000,
		        fixed: true
		    },
		    style: {
		        classes: "qtip-light"
		    }
		})

            // Make sure it doesn't follow the link when we click it
        });
    });
</script>
